5/6/22, 19:26 - ğŸ¦: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>

CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

int ma_265_handler = 0;
int ma_11_handler = 0;
int rsi_2_handler = 0;

ulong trade_ticket = 0;
bool time_passed = true;

double ma_265_array[];
double ma_11_array[];
double rsi_2_array[];
double ma_11_close_pos[];

double stop = 0;

double candle_close;
double prev_close;
datetime time_candle;


double current_open;
double prev_open;

bool done = false;

int OnInit() {
   ma_265_handler = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, 265, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_CLOSE);
   ma_11_handler = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, 11, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_CLOSE);
   rsi_2_handler = iRSI(_Symbol, _Period, 2, PRICE_CLOSE);

   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}

void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_265_handler, 0, 1, 1, ma_265_array);
   CopyBuffer(ma_11_handler, 0, 1, 1, ma_11_array);
   CopyBuffer(rsi_2_handler, 0, 1, 2, rsi_2_array);
   
   candle_close = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   
   if (time_passed == false) return;
   if (!PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) trade_ticket = 0;
   if (trade_ticket > 0) {
      CopyBuffer(ma_11_handler, 0, 1, 2, ma_11_close_pos);
      current_open = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
      prev_open = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 2);
      /* CLOSING POSITIONS */
      if (
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
            && prev_open > ma_11_close_pos[1]
            && current_open < ma_11_close_pos[0]
         ) ||
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
            && prev_open < ma_11_close_pos[1]
            && current_open > ma_11_close_pos[0]
         )
      ) {
         Comment(
            "Position type ", pos_info.PositionType(),
            "\n",
            "Price open ", pos_info.PriceOpen()
         );
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket);  
      }
   } else {
      /* OPENING POSITIONS */
      if (
         // buy
         (
            candle_close > ma_265_array[0]
            && candle_close < ma_11_array[0]
            && (
               rsi_2_array[0] < 25
               && rsi_2_array[1] > rsi_2_array[0]
               && rsi_2_array[1] > 25
            )
         )
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);   
         trade.Buy(1, _Symbol, Ask, Ask - (Ask * 0.005)); // TODO: SET STOP
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(600);
      } else if (
         // sell
         (
            candle_close < ma_265_array[0]
            && candle_close > ma_11_array[0]
            && (
               rsi_2_array[0] > 75
               && rsi_2_array[1] < rsi_2_array[0]
               && rsi_2_array[1] < 75
            )
         )
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         trade.Sell(1, _Symbol, Bid, Bid + (Bid * 0.005)); // TODO: SET STOP
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(600);
      }
   } 
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

12/6/22, 17:06 - ğŸ¦: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>

CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

int ao_handler = 0;
double ao_array[];
double ao_array_trade[];
double STOP_MULTIPLIER = 0.5;

int atr_14_handler = 0;
double atr_14_array[];

ulong trade_ticket = 0;
bool time_passed = true;
datetime time_candle;
uint state = 9;

uint GREEN = 1;
uint RED = 0;
bool can_trade = true;
double diff = 0;
uint SECONDS = 300;

int OnInit() {
   ao_handler = iCustom(_Symbol, _Period, "../Indicators/Examples/Awesome_Oscillator_2");
   atr_14_handler = iATR(_Symbol, _Period, 14);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}

void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ao_handler, 0, 1, 2, ao_array);
   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   if (time_passed == false) return;
   if (!PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) trade_ticket = 0;

   if (trade_ticket > 0) {
      if (
         pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
         && ao_array[1] > ao_array[0]
         && state == RED
      ) {
         state = GREEN;
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket); 
      } else if (
         pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
         && ao_array[1] < ao_array[0]
         && state == GREEN
      ) {
         state = RED;
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket); 
      }
   } else {
      double Ask_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
      double Bid_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
      diff = Ask_op - Bid_op;

      CopyBuffer(ao_handler, 0, 1, 3, ao_array_trade);
      if (
         (
            ao_array_trade[1] <= 0
            && ao_array_trade[0] > 0
         )
         ||
         (
            ao_array_trade[1] >= 0
            && ao_array_trade[0] < 0
         )
         ||
         (
            (
               ao_array_trade[0] < 0
               && ao_array_trade[1] < 0
               && ao_array_trade[2] < 0 
            ) &&
            (
               (
                  ao_array_trade[2] > ao_array_trade[1]
                  && ao_array_trade[1] < ao_array_trade[0]
               ) ||
               (
                  ao_array_trade[2] < ao_array_trade[1]
                  && ao_array_trade[1] > ao_array_trade[0]
               )
            )
         )
         ||
         (
            (
               ao_array_trade[0] > 0
               && ao_array_trade[1] > 0
               && ao_array_trade[2] > 0 
            ) &&
            (
               (
                  ao_array_trade[2] > ao_array_trade[1]
                  && ao_array_trade[1] < ao_array_trade[0]
               ) ||
               (
                  ao_array_trade[2] < ao_array_trade[1]
                  && ao_array_trade[1] > ao_array_trade[0]
               )
            )
         )
      ) {
         if(diff > 1) {
            can_trade = false;
         } else {
            can_trade = true;
         }
      }

      if (can_trade == false) return;
      CopyBuffer(atr_14_handler, 0, 1, 1, atr_14_array);
      if (
         (
            ao_array[1] <= 0
            && ao_array[0] > 0
         )
         ||
         (
            ao_array[0] < 0
            && ao_array[1] < 0
            && ao_array[1] < ao_array[0]
            && state == GREEN
         )
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         trade.Sell(1, _Symbol, Bid, Bid + (atr_14_array[0] * STOP_MULTIPLIER));
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(SECONDS);
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) {
            state = RED;
         }
         can_trade = false;
      } else if (
         (
            ao_array[1] >= 0
            && ao_array[0] < 0
         )
         ||
         (
            ao_array[0] > 0
            && ao_array[1] > 0
            && ao_array[1] > ao_array[0]
            && state == RED
         )
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);   
         trade.Buy(1, _Symbol, Ask, Ask - (atr_14_array[0] * STOP_MULTIPLIER));
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(SECONDS);
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) {
            state = GREEN;
         }
         can_trade = false;
      }
   }
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//|                                          Export Indicator Values |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
#property description "This Script Export Indicators Values to CSV File."
#property description "(You can change the iCustom function parameters to change what indicator to export)"
#property copyright "NFTrader"
#property version   "2.00"
#property script_show_inputs

input int    IndicatorPeriod=14;
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Script program start function                                    |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
void OnStart()
  {
   MqlRates  rates_array[];
   string sSymbol=Symbol();
   string  sPeriod=EnumToString(Period());

   ArraySetAsSeries(rates_array,true);
   int MaxBar=TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_MAXBARS);
   int iCurrent=CopyRates(sSymbol,Period(),0,MaxBar,rates_array);

   double ZeroIndicatorBuffer[];
   double FirstIndicatorBuffer[];
   SetIndexBuffer(0,ZeroIndicatorBuffer,INDICATOR_DATA);
   SetIndexBuffer(0,FirstIndicatorBuffer,INDICATOR_DATA);

   int to_copy = Bars(sSymbol,PERIOD_CURRENT);
   int zeroZigZag = iCustom(_Symbol, _Period, "../Indicators/Examples/ZigzagColor");
   int firstZigZag = iCustom(_Symbol, _Period, "../Indicators/Examples/ZigzagColor");

   CopyBuffer(zeroZigZag, 0, 0, to_copy, ZeroIndicatorBuffer);
   CopyBuffer(firstZigZag, 1, 0, to_copy, FirstIndicatorBuffer);
   ArraySetAsSeries(ZeroIndicatorBuffer, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(FirstIndicatorBuffer, true);

   int fileHandle=FileOpen("indicator_data.csv",FILE_WRITE|FILE_CSV);

   for(int i = iCurrent-IndicatorPeriod-1; i > 0; i--)
     {
      string outputData=StringFormat("%s",TimeToString(rates_array[i].time,TIME_DATE));
      outputData += "," + TimeToString(rates_array[i].time,TIME_MINUTES);
      outputData += "," + (string)rates_array[i].high;
      outputData += "," + (string)rates_array[i].open;
      outputData += "," + (string)rates_array[i].close;
      outputData += "," + (string)rates_array[i].low;
      outputData += "," + DoubleToString(ZeroIndicatorBuffer[i], 2);
      outputData += "," + DoubleToString(FirstIndicatorBuffer[i], 2);
      outputData += "\n";

      FileWriteString(fileHandle,outputData);
     }

   FileClose(fileHandle);
   Comment(fileHandle);
  }
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

18/9/22, 21:26 - ğŸ¦: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>

CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

ulong ticket_buy = 0;
ulong ticket_sell = 0;

bool time_passed = true;
datetime time_candle;

int ma_1_handler = 0;
int bol_bands_handler = 0;

double ma_1_array[];
double bol_bands_base[];
double bol_bands_upper[];
double bol_bands_lower[];

double profit = 0;
double diff = 0;

// SPREAD, SI ES 1 SON 100 PUNTOS
double SPREAD = 1.5;
// SEGUNDOS DEPENDIENDO DEL MARCO TEMPORAL EJ: 1800 SEGUNDOS SON VELAS DE 30MIN EN SEGUNDOS
uint TIME_FRAME = 1800;
// VOLUMEN DE LA TRANSACCION
double VOLUME = 0.1;
uint BOLLINGER_PERIODS = 90;
double STANDARD_DEVIATIONS = 0.5;


int OnInit() {
   ma_1_handler = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, 1, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE);
   bol_bands_handler = iBands(_Symbol, _Period, BOLLINGER_PERIODS, 0, STANDARD_DEVIATIONS, PRICE_CLOSE);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}


void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_1_handler, 0, 1, 2, ma_1_array);
   CopyBuffer(bol_bands_handler, 0, 1, 2, bol_bands_base);
   CopyBuffer(bol_bands_handler, 1, 1, 1, bol_bands_upper);
   CopyBuffer(bol_bands_handler, 2, 1, 1, bol_bands_lower);

   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

   double Ask_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   double Bid_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   diff = Ask_op - Bid_op;

   if (time_passed == false) return;

   if(!pos_info.SelectByTicket(ticket_sell)) ticket_sell = 0;
   if(
      ma_1_array[0] < bol_bands_base[0]
      && ma_1_array[1] > bol_bands_base[1]
      && ticket_sell > 0
      && pos_info.PriceOpen() > ma_1_array[1]
      && pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
   ) {
      trade.PositionClose(ticket_sell);
      Print("RESULTADO DE LA TRANSACCION: ", trade.ResultRetcode());
      if (trade.ResultRetcode() == TRADE_RETCODE_DONE) {
         ticket_sell = 0;
      }
   } 
   
   if(!pos_info.SelectByTicket(ticket_buy)) ticket_buy = 0;
   if(
      ma_1_array[0] > bol_bands_base[0]
      && ma_1_array[1] < bol_bands_base[1]
      && ticket_buy > 0
      && pos_info.PriceOpen() < ma_1_array[1]
      && pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
   ) {
      trade.PositionClose(ticket_buy);
      if (trade.ResultRetcode() == TRADE_RETCODE_DONE) {
         ticket_buy = 0;
      }
   }

   if (
      ma_1_array[0] < bol_bands_base[0]
      && ma_1_array[1] > bol_bands_base[1]
      && diff <= SPREAD
      && ticket_buy == 0
   ) {
      double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
      trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, Ask, bol_bands_lower[0]); // 0.
      ticket_buy = trade.ResultOrder();
      time_passed = false;
      EventSetTimer(TIME_FRAME);
   } else if (
      ma_1_array[0] > bol_bands_base[0]
      && ma_1_array[1] < bol_bands_base[1]
      && diff <= SPREAD
      && ticket_sell == 0
   ) {
      double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
      trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, Bid, bol_bands_upper[0]);
      ticket_sell = trade.ResultOrder();
      time_passed = false;
      EventSetTimer(TIME_FRAME);
   }

}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

//|                                                      b-clock.mq5 |
//|                                Copyright 2013, Totom Sukopratomo |
//|                        https://login.mql5.com/en/users/tomsuk001 |
//|                                      totom.sukopratomo@yahoo.com |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//|                                                   Convert from : |
//+--------                                                          +
//|                                                      b-clock.mq4 |
//|                                     Core time code by Nick Bilak |
//|        http://metatrader.50webs.com/         beluck[at]gmail.com |
//|                                  modified by adoleh2000 and dwt5 | 
//+-----                                                             +
//|        Original MQL4 code found at: http://codebase.mql4.com/590 |

#property copyright "Copyright 2013, Totom Sukopratomo"
#property link      "https://login.mql5.com/en/users/tomsuk001"
#property version   "2.00"
#property indicator_chart_window
//--- input parameters
input bool     ShowComment=true;
input color    FontColor=clrDarkGray;
input int      FontSize=10;
input string   FontName="Tahoma";
input int      Offset=5;
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Custom indicator initialization function                         |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
int OnInit()
  {
//--- indicator buffers mapping

//---
   return(0);
  }
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Custom indicator deinitialization function                        |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
void OnDeinit(const int reason)
  {
   Comment("");
   ObjectDelete(0,"time");
  }
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Custom indicator iteration function                              |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
int OnCalculate(const int rates_total,
                const int prev_calculated,
                const int begin,
                const double &price[])
  {
   MqlRates rates[];
   MqlTick tick;
   SymbolInfoTick(Symbol(),tick);
   if(CopyRates(Symbol(),PERIOD_CURRENT,0,1,rates)<1)return(0);
   double i;
   long m,s;
   m=rates[0].time+GetMinute()*60-tick.time;
   i=m/60.0;
   s=m%60;
   m=(m-m%60)/60;

   if(ShowComment)
      Comment(IntegerToString(m,0,' ')+" minutes "+IntegerToString(s,0,' ')+" seconds left to bar end");

   string text="  <"+IntegerToString(m,0,' ')+":"+IntegerToString(s,0,' ');
   if(ObjectFind(0,"time")<1)
     {
      ObjectCreate(0,"time",OBJ_TEXT,0,rates[0].time,tick.bid+Point()*Offset);
      ObjectSetString(0,"time",OBJPROP_TEXT,text);
      ObjectSetInteger(0,"time",OBJPROP_COLOR,FontColor);
      ObjectSetInteger(0,"time",OBJPROP_FONTSIZE,FontSize);
      ObjectSetString(0,"time",OBJPROP_FONT,FontName);
     }
   else
     {
      ObjectSetString(0,"time",OBJPROP_TEXT,text);
      ObjectMove(0,"time",0,rates[0].time,tick.bid+Point()*Offset);
     }
//---

//--- return value of prev_calculated for next call
   return(rates_total);
  }
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

int GetMinute()
  {
   switch(Period())
     {
      case PERIOD_M1: return(1);
      case PERIOD_M2: return(2);
      case PERIOD_M3: return(3);
      case PERIOD_M4: return(4);
      case PERIOD_M5: return(5);
      case PERIOD_M6: return(6);
      case PERIOD_M10: return(10);
      case PERIOD_M12: return(12);
      case PERIOD_M15: return(15);
      case PERIOD_M20: return(20);
      case PERIOD_M30: return(30);
      case PERIOD_H1: return(60);
      case PERIOD_H2: return(120);
      case PERIOD_H3: return(180);
      case PERIOD_H4: return(240);
      case PERIOD_H6: return(360);
      case PERIOD_H8: return(480);
      case PERIOD_H12: return(720);
      case PERIOD_D1: return(1440);
      case PERIOD_W1: return(10080);
      case PERIOD_MN1: return(43200);
     }
   return(1);
  }
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

10/10/22, 23:26 - ğŸ¦: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>
 
CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

bool time_passed = true;
ulong trade_ticket = 0;
bool first_position = true;
double initial_price = 0.0;
double brick_size = 0.0;
uint BRICK_BOX_VALUE = 500;
double VOLUME = 0.1;
double point = 0.0;
double diff = 0.0;
uint SPREAD = 100;

uint last_type;
double last_sl;
double last_tp;

int OnInit() {
   point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
   brick_size = BRICK_BOX_VALUE * point;
   initial_price = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}

void OnTick() {
   double bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   double ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   diff = ask - bid;

   if (diff >= SPREAD) return;
   if (first_position) {
        if((bid - initial_price) >= brick_size) {
            trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, ask, bid - brick_size, bid + brick_size);
            last_sl = bid - brick_size;
            last_tp = bid + brick_size;
            last_type = POSITION_TYPE_BUY;
        } else if ((initial_price - bid) >= brick_size) {
            trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, bid, bid + brick_size, bid - brick_size);
            last_sl = bid + brick_size;
            last_tp = bid - brick_size;
            last_type = POSITION_TYPE_SELL;
        }
        if (trade.ResultRetcode() == TRADE_RETCODE_DONE) {
            first_position = false;
        }
   } else {
      uint pos_type = last_type;
      double pos_profit = last_tp;
      double pos_stop = last_sl;

      if (pos_type == POSITION_TYPE_BUY && bid > pos_profit) {
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, ask, bid - brick_size, bid + brick_size);
         last_sl = bid - brick_size;
         last_tp = bid + brick_size;
         last_type = POSITION_TYPE_BUY;
      } else if (pos_type == POSITION_TYPE_BUY && bid < pos_stop) {
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, bid, bid + brick_size, bid - brick_size);
         last_sl = bid - brick_size;
         last_tp = bid + brick_size;
         last_type = POSITION_TYPE_BUY;
      } else if (pos_type == POSITION_TYPE_SELL && bid < pos_profit) {
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, bid, bid + brick_size, bid - brick_size);
         last_sl = bid + brick_size;
         last_tp = bid - brick_size;
         last_type = POSITION_TYPE_SELL;
      } else if (pos_type == POSITION_TYPE_SELL && bid > pos_stop) {
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, ask, bid - brick_size, bid + brick_size);
         last_sl = bid + brick_size;
         last_tp = bid - brick_size;
         last_type = POSITION_TYPE_SELL;
      }
      if (trade.ResultRetcode() != TRADE_RETCODE_DONE) {
         first_position = true;
         initial_price = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
      }
   }
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>
 
CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

bool time_passed = true;
ulong trade_ticket = 0;
bool first_position = true;
double initial_price = 0.0;
double brick_size = 0.0;
uint BRICK_BOX_VALUE = 5000;
double VOLUME = 0.1;
double point = 0.0;
double spread = 0.0;
uint SPREAD = 100;

uint last_type;
double last_sl;
double last_tp;

int OnInit() {
   point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
   brick_size = BRICK_BOX_VALUE * point;
   initial_price = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}

void OnTick() {
   double bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   double ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   spread = ask - bid;

   if (spread >= SPREAD) return;
   if (first_position) {
        if(bid >= (initial_price + brick_size - spread)) {
            trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, 0, ask - brick_size, bid + brick_size);
            last_sl = ask - brick_size;
            last_tp = bid + brick_size;
            last_type = POSITION_TYPE_BUY;
        } else if (ask <= (initial_price - brick_size + spread)) {
            trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, 0, bid + brick_size, ask - brick_size);
            last_sl = bid + brick_size;
            last_tp = ask - brick_size;
            last_type = POSITION_TYPE_SELL;
        }
        if (trade.ResultRetcode() == TRADE_RETCODE_DONE) {
            first_position = false;
        }
   } else {
      if (last_type == POSITION_TYPE_BUY && bid >= last_tp) {
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, 0, ask - brick_size, bid + brick_size);
         last_sl = ask - brick_size;
         last_tp = bid + brick_size;
         last_type = POSITION_TYPE_BUY;
      } else if (last_type == POSITION_TYPE_BUY && bid <= last_sl) {
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, 0, bid + brick_size, ask - brick_size);
         last_sl = bid + brick_size;
         last_tp = ask - brick_size;
         last_type = POSITION_TYPE_SELL;
      } else if (last_type == POSITION_TYPE_SELL && ask <= last_tp) {
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, 0, bid + brick_size, ask - brick_size);
         last_sl = bid + brick_size;
         last_tp = ask - brick_size;
         last_type = POSITION_TYPE_SELL;
      } else if (last_type == POSITION_TYPE_SELL && ask >= last_sl) {
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, 0, ask - brick_size, bid + brick_size);
         last_sl = ask - brick_size;
         last_tp = bid + brick_size;
         last_type = POSITION_TYPE_BUY;
      }
      if (trade.ResultRetcode() != TRADE_RETCODE_DONE) {
         first_position = true;
         initial_price = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
      }
   }
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

            last_tp = ask - brick_size;
            last_type = POSITION_TYPE_SELL;
         } else if (last_type == POSITION_TYPE_SELL && ask <= last_tp) {
            trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, 0, bid + brick_size, ask - brick_size);
            last_sl = bid + brick_size;
            last_tp = ask - brick_size;
            last_type = POSITION_TYPE_SELL;
         } else if (last_type == POSITION_TYPE_SELL && ask >= last_sl) {
            trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, 0, ask - brick_size, bid + brick_size);
            last_sl = ask - brick_size;
            last_tp = bid + brick_size;
            last_type = POSITION_TYPE_BUY;
         }
         if (trade.ResultRetcode() != TRADE_RETCODE_DONE) {
            first_position = true;
            initial_price = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         }
      }
   }
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

20/10/22, 15:24 - ğŸ¦: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>

CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

ulong trade_ticket = 0;
bool time_passed = true;
datetime time_candle;
double last_close = 0;

uint MEAN_PERIODS = 10000;
uint CANDLE_STICK = 60;
uint STOP = 20;
double VOLUME = 0.1;

int ma_handler_high = 0;
int ma_handler_low = 0;
int ma_1_handler = 0;

double ma_high_array[];
double ma_low_array[];

bool limit_low;
bool limit_high;

int OnInit() {
   ma_handler_high = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_HIGH);
   ma_handler_low = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_LOW);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}


void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_high, 0, 1, 2, ma_high_array);
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_low, 0, 1, 2, ma_low_array);

   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_close = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

   if (time_candle == StringToTime("2022.09.01 04:32")) {
      Print("hola");
   }

   if (time_passed == false) return;
   if (!PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) trade_ticket = 0;
   if (trade_ticket > 0) {
      if (
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
            && limit_low == true
            && last_close > ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close > ma_high_array[1]
         )
         ||
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
            && limit_high == true
            && last_close < ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close < ma_high_array[1]
         )
      ) {
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket);
      }
   }
   if (trade_ticket == 0) {
      if (
         limit_low == true
         && last_close > ma_low_array[1]
         && last_close > ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);   
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, Ask, Ask - STOP);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_low = false;
      }
      if (
         limit_high == true
         && last_close < ma_low_array[1]
         && last_close < ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, Bid, Bid + STOP);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_high = false;
      }
   }
   
   if (last_close < ma_low_array[1]) {
      limit_low = true;
   } else if (
      last_close > ma_high_array[1]
   ) {
      limit_high = true;
   }
   /*Comment(
      "limit_low ", limit_low, "\n",
      "limit_high ", limit_high, "\n",
      "ma_low_array[1] ", ma_low_array[1], "\n",
      "ma_high_array[1] ", ma_high_array[1], "\n"
   );*/
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

26/10/22, 13:59 - Jhon Edward Sanz: from cmath import nan
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np



velas = pd.read_csv("US100M30.csv", sep="\t")
point = 0.01
periodos = 380

#formato
velas["<VELA>"] = np.where(velas["<CLOSE>"]-velas["<OPEN>"]>0, "+", "-")
velas["<BID>"] = velas["<CLOSE>"]
velas["<ASK>"] = velas["<CLOSE>"] + (velas["<SPREAD>"]*point)


velas["<MediaMovil>"] = velas["<CLOSE>"].rolling(periodos).mean()
velas = velas.reindex(columns=["<DATE>","<TIME>","<SPREAD>","<HIGH>","<LOW>","<OPEN>","<BID>","<ASK>","<VELA>", "<MediaMovil>"])

#imprime las velas
#print(velas)


operaciones = {"date_in": [], "time_in": [], "in": [], "type": [] ,"date_out": [], "time_out": [], "out": [], "profit": []}
compra, venta, stop = 0, 0, 0
tipo, date_in, time_in, date_out, time_out = "","","","",""
numero_stops = 0

for i in range(len(velas)):

    #compra
    if compra == 0 and velas.loc[i,"<MediaMovil>"] != nan and velas.loc[i,"<LOW>"] > velas.loc[i,"<MediaMovil>"] and velas.loc[i,"<VELA>"] == "+" and tipo == "":
        compra = velas.loc[i,"<ASK>"]
        stop = velas.loc[i,"<LOW>"]
        date_in = velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"]
        time_in = velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"]
        tipo = "compra"
        #print("se hace la compra", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
       
    #gana la compra
    elif tipo == "compra" and velas.loc[i,"<BID>"]-compra > 0 and velas.loc[i,"<LOW>"] > stop:
        operaciones["date_in"].append(date_in)
        operaciones["time_in"].append(time_in)
        operaciones["in"].append(compra)
        operaciones["type"].append(tipo)
        operaciones["date_out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"])
        operaciones["time_out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        operaciones["out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<BID>"])
        operaciones["profit"].append(velas.loc[i,"<BID>"] - compra)
        #print("se agrega la compra ganando", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])

        if velas.loc[i,"<LOW>"] > velas.loc[i,"<MediaMovil>"] and velas.loc[i,"<VELA>"] == "+":
            compra = velas.loc[i,"<ASK>"]
            stop = velas.loc[i,"<LOW>"]
            date_in = velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"]
            time_in = velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"]
            tipo = "compra"
            date_out, time_out = "",""
            #print("se comprueba si se puede hacer otra compra", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        
        else:
            compra, venta, stop = 0, 0, 0
            tipo, date_in, time_in, date_out, time_out = "","","","",""
            #print("vuelve a empezar", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])

    #pierde la compra    
    elif velas.loc[i,"<LOW>"] <= stop and tipo == "compra":
        operaciones["date_in"].append(date_in)
        operaciones["time_in"].append(time_in)
        operaciones["in"].append(compra)
        operaciones["type"].append(tipo)
        operaciones["date_out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"])
        operaciones["time_out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        operaciones["out"].append(stop)
        operaciones["profit"].append(stop-compra)
        numero_stops += 1
        #print("se agrega la compra perdiedo", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        
        if velas.loc[i,"<LOW>"] > velas.loc[i,"<MediaMovil>"] and velas.loc[i,"<VELA>"] == "+":
            compra = velas.loc[i,"<ASK>"]
            stop = velas.loc[i,"<LOW>"]
            date_in = velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"]
            time_in = velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"]
            tipo = "compra"
            date_out, time_out = "",""
            #print("se comprueba si se puede hacer otra compra despues del stop", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        
        else:
            compra, venta, stop = 0, 0, 0
            tipo, date_in, time_in, date_out, time_out = "","","","",""
            #print("vuelve a empezar despues del stop", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
                 

    #venta
    if venta == 0 and velas.loc[i,"<MediaMovil>"] != nan and velas.loc[i,"<HIGH>"] < velas.loc[i,"<MediaMovil>"] and velas.loc[i,"<VELA>"] == "-" and tipo == "":
        venta = velas.loc[i,"<BID>"]
        stop = velas.loc[i,"<HIGH>"]
        date_in = velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"]
        time_in = velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"]
        tipo = "venta"
        #print("se hace la venta", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
    
    #gana la venta
    elif tipo == "venta" and venta-velas.loc[i,"<ASK>"] > 0 and velas.loc[i,"<HIGH>"] < stop:
        operaciones["date_in"].append(date_in)
        operaciones["time_in"].append(time_in)
        operaciones["in"].append(venta)
        operaciones["type"].append(tipo)
        operaciones["date_out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"])
        operaciones["time_out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        operaciones["out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<BID>"])
        operaciones["profit"].append(venta - velas.loc[i,"<ASK>"])
        #print("se agrega la venta ganando", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])

        if velas.loc[i,"<HIGH>"] < velas.loc[i,"<MediaMovil>"] and velas.loc[i,"<VELA>"] == "-":
            venta = velas.loc[i,"<BID>"]
            stop = velas.loc[i,"<HIGH>"]
            date_in = velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"]
            time_in = velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"]
            tipo = "venta"
            date_out, time_out = "",""
            #print("se comprueba si se puede hacer otra venta", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        
        else:
            venta, venta, stop = 0, 0, 0
            tipo, date_in, time_in, date_out, time_out = "","","","",""
            #print("vuelve a empezar", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])

    #pierde la venta    
    elif velas.loc[i,"<HIGH>"] >= stop and tipo == "venta":
        operaciones["date_in"].append(date_in)
        operaciones["time_in"].append(time_in)
        operaciones["in"].append(venta)
        operaciones["type"].append(tipo)
        operaciones["date_out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"])
        operaciones["time_out"].append(velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        operaciones["out"].append(stop)
        operaciones["profit"].append(venta-stop)
        numero_stops += 1
        #print("se agrega la venta perdiedo", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        
        if velas.loc[i,"<HIGH>"] < velas.loc[i,"<MediaMovil>"] and velas.loc[i,"<VELA>"] == "-":
            venta = velas.loc[i,"<BID>"]
            stop = velas.loc[i,"<HIGH>"]
            date_in = velas.loc[i,"<DATE>"]
            time_in = velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"]
            tipo = "venta"
            date_out, time_out = "",""
            #print("se comprueba si se puede hacer otra venta despues del stop", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])
        
        else:
            venta, venta, stop = 0, 0, 0
            tipo, date_in, time_in, date_out, time_out = "","","","",""
            #print("vuelve a empezar despues del stop", velas.loc[i,"<TIME>"])



    
#operaciones y acumulado
resultados = pd.DataFrame(operaciones)
acumulado = operaciones["acumulado"] = np.cumsum(resultados["profit"])
resultados["acumulado"] = acumulado
print()
print(resultados.iloc[200:250])


#estadisticas
num_trades = len(resultados)
numero_stops = numero_stops
total_profit = resultados["profit"].sum()

porcent_ganados = resultados[resultados["profit"]>0].count()
porcent_ganados = (porcent_ganados["profit"]/num_trades)*100
porcent_perdidos = resultados[resultados["profit"]<0].count()
porcent_perdidos = (porcent_perdidos["profit"]/num_trades)*100

promedio_ganadas = resultados[resultados["profit"]>0].mean(numeric_only=True)
promedio_perdidas = resultados[resultados["profit"]<0].mean(numeric_only=True)

em =((porcent_ganados*promedio_ganadas["profit"])-(porcent_perdidos*promedio_perdidas["profit"]))/100

peor_operacion = resultados["profit"].min()
mejor_operacion = resultados["profit"].max()



print()
estadisticas = pd.Series([num_trades, numero_stops, total_profit, porcent_ganados, porcent_perdidos, promedio_ganadas["profit"], promedio_perdidas["profit"], em, peor_operacion, mejor_operacion  ], 
                index=   ["numero de trades:", "numero de stops:", "total profit","% ganados", "% perdidas", "promedio ganados", "promedio perdidos", "EM","peor operacion", "mejor operacion"])

print(estadisticas)

28/10/22, 16:17 - ğŸ¦: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>

CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

ulong trade_ticket = 0;
bool time_passed = true;
datetime time_candle;
double last_close = 0;
double last_low = 0;
double last_high = 0;

uint MEAN_PERIODS = 500;
uint CANDLE_STICK = 60 * 10;
uint STOP = 20;
double VOLUME = 0.1;
double LIMIT_STOP = 200;

int ma_handler_high = 0;
int ma_handler_low = 0;
int ma_1_handler = 0;

double ma_high_array[];
double ma_low_array[];

bool limit_low;
bool limit_high;
double diff = 0;
double SPREAD = 1;

int OnInit() {
   ma_handler_high = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_HIGH);
   ma_handler_low = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_LOW);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}


void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_high, 0, 1, 2, ma_high_array);
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_low, 0, 1, 2, ma_low_array);

   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_close = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_low = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_high = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

   double Ask_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   double Bid_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   diff = Ask_op - Bid_op;

   if (time_passed == false) return;
   if (!PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) trade_ticket = 0;
   if (trade_ticket > 0) {
      if (
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
            && limit_low == true
            && last_close > ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close > ma_high_array[1]
         )
         ||
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
            && limit_high == true
            && last_close < ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close < ma_high_array[1]
         )
      ) {
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket);
      }
   }
   if (trade_ticket == 0) {
      if (
         limit_low == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_low > ma_low_array[1]
         && last_low > ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         if (Ask -  ma_low_array[1] > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Ask - LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_low_array[1];
         }
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, Ask, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_low = false;
      }
      if (
         limit_high == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_high < ma_low_array[1]
         && last_high < ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         if (ma_high_array[1] - Bid > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Bid + LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_high_array[1];
         }
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, Bid, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_high = false;
      }
   }
   
   if (last_close < ma_low_array[1]) {
      limit_low = true;
   } else if (
      last_close > ma_high_array[1]
   ) {
      limit_high = true;
   }
   /*Comment(
      "limit_low ", limit_low, "\n",
      "limit_high ", limit_high, "\n",
      "ma_low_array[1] ", ma_low_array[1], "\n",
      "ma_high_array[1] ", ma_high_array[1], "\n"
   );*/
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

bool limit_high;
double diff = 0;
double SPREAD = 1;
double point = 0.0;

int OnInit() {
   point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
   SPREAD = SPREAD * point;
   LIMIT_STOP = LIMIT_STOP * point;
   ma_handler_high = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_HIGH);
   ma_handler_low = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_LOW);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}


void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_high, 0, 1, 2, ma_high_array);
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_low, 0, 1, 2, ma_low_array);

   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_close = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_low = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_high = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

   double Ask_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   double Bid_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   diff = Ask_op - Bid_op;

   if (time_passed == false) return;
   if (!PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) trade_ticket = 0;
   if (trade_ticket > 0) {
      if (
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
            && limit_low == true
            && last_close > ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close > ma_high_array[1]
         )
         ||
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
            && limit_high == true
            && last_close < ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close < ma_high_array[1]
         )
      ) {
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket);
      }
   }
   if (trade_ticket == 0) {
      if (
         limit_low == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_low > ma_low_array[1]
         && last_low > ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         if (Ask -  ma_low_array[1] > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Ask - LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_low_array[1];
         }
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, Ask, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_low = false;
      }
      if (
         limit_high == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_high < ma_low_array[1]
         && last_high < ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         if (ma_high_array[1] - Bid > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Bid + LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_high_array[1];
         }
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, Bid, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_high = false;
      }
   }
   
   if (last_close < ma_low_array[1]) {
      limit_low = true;
   } else if (
      last_close > ma_high_array[1]
   ) {
      limit_high = true;
   }
   /*Comment(
      "limit_low ", limit_low, "\n",
      "limit_high ", limit_high, "\n",
      "ma_low_array[1] ", ma_low_array[1], "\n",
      "ma_high_array[1] ", ma_high_array[1], "\n"
   );*/
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

//|                                                       StdDev.mq5 |
//|                   Copyright 2009-2020, MetaQuotes Software Corp. |
//|                                              http://www.mql5.com |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
#property copyright   "2009-2020, MetaQuotes Software Corp."
#property link        "http://www.mql5.com"
#property description "Standard Deviation"

#property indicator_separate_window
#property indicator_buffers 2
#property indicator_plots   1
#property indicator_type1   DRAW_LINE
#property indicator_color1  MediumSeaGreen
#property indicator_style1  STYLE_SOLID

input int InpMidCandlePeriod = 20;
double ExtMidCandleBuffer[];
int MidCandlePeriod;

void OnInit() {
   if(InpMidCandlePeriod <= 1) {
      MidCandlePeriod = 20;
      PrintFormat(
         "Incorrect value for input variable InpMidCandlePeriod=%d. Indicator will use value %d for calculations.",
         InpMidCandlePeriod,MidCandlePeriod
      );
   } else {
      MidCandlePeriod=InpMidCandlePeriod;
   }

   SetIndexBuffer(0,ExtMidCandleBuffer);
   string short_name = StringFormat("MidCandle (%d)",MidCandlePeriod);
   IndicatorSetString(INDICATOR_SHORTNAME, short_name);
   PlotIndexSetString(0, PLOT_LABEL, short_name);
}

int OnCalculate(
   const int rates_total,
   const int prev_calculated,
   const datetime &time[],
   const double &open[],
   const double &high[],
   const double &low[],
   const double &close[],
   const long &tick_volume[],
   const long &volume[],
   const int &spread[]
) {
   if(rates_total < MidCandlePeriod)
      return(0);

   int start = prev_calculated - 1;
   if(start < MidCandlePeriod) {
      start = MidCandlePeriod - 1;
      ArrayInitialize(ExtMidCandleBuffer, 0.0);
      PlotIndexSetInteger(0, PLOT_DRAW_BEGIN, MidCandlePeriod - 1);
   }

   for(int i = start; i < rates_total && !IsStopped(); i++) {
      ExtMidCandleBuffer[i] = MidCandleFunc(open, close, i);
   }
   return(rates_total);
}

double CalcMid(
   const double &top[],
   const double &bottom[],
   const int position
) {
   double diff = MathAbs(top[position] - bottom[position]) / 2;
   double mid = 0.0;
   if (top[position] > bottom[position]) {
      mid = bottom[position] + diff;
   } else {
      mid = bottom[position] - diff;
   }
   return mid;
}

double MidCandleFunc(
   const double &open[],
   const double &close[],
   const int position
) {
   /*
   double dev=0.0;
   for(int i = 0; i < MidCandlePeriod; i++)
      dev += MathPow(price[position-i]-ma_price[position], 2.0);
   dev = MathSqrt(dev/MidCandlePeriod);
   */
   double currentCandle = CalcMid(open, close, position);
   double prevCandle = CalcMid(open, close, position - 1);
   return MathAbs(currentCandle - prevCandle);
}
10/11/22, 13:30 - ğŸ¦: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>

CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

ulong trade_ticket = 0;
bool time_passed = true;
datetime time_candle;
double last_close = 0;
double last_low = 0;
double last_high = 0;

uint MEAN_PERIODS = 395;
uint CANDLE_STICK = 60 * 10;
double VOLUME = 0.1;
double LIMIT_STOP = 20; // puntos

int ma_handler_high = 0;
int ma_handler_low = 0;
int ma_1_handler = 0;

double ma_high_array[];
double ma_low_array[];

bool limit_low;
bool limit_high;
double diff = 0;
double SPREAD = 10;
double point = 0.0;

int OnInit() {
   point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
   SPREAD = SPREAD * point;
   LIMIT_STOP = LIMIT_STOP * point;
   ma_handler_high = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_HIGH);
   ma_handler_low = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_LOW);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}


void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_high, 0, 1, 2, ma_high_array);
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_low, 0, 1, 2, ma_low_array);

   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_close = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_low = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_high = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

   double Ask_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   double Bid_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   diff = Ask_op - Bid_op;

   datetime start = TimeCurrent();
   datetime compilation_time=__DATETIME__-__DATE__;
    
   MqlDateTime rightNow;
   TimeCurrent(rightNow);
   TimeToStruct(TimeCurrent(),rightNow);
   if (!(rightNow.hour > 2 && rightNow.hour < 22)) return;

   if (time_passed == false) return;
   if (!PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) trade_ticket = 0;
   if (trade_ticket > 0) {
      if (
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
            && limit_low == true
            && last_close > ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close > ma_high_array[1]
         )
         ||
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
            && limit_high == true
            && last_close < ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close < ma_high_array[1]
         )
      ) {
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket);
      }
   }
   if (trade_ticket == 0) {
      if (
         limit_low == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_low > ma_low_array[1]
         && last_low > ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         if (Ask -  ma_low_array[1] > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Ask - LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_low_array[1];
         }
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, Ask, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_low = false;
      }
      if (
         limit_high == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_high < ma_low_array[1]
         && last_high < ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         if (ma_high_array[1] - Bid > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Bid + LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_high_array[1];
         }
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, Bid, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_high = false;
      }
   }
   
   if (last_close < ma_low_array[1]) {
      limit_low = true;
   } else if (
      last_close > ma_high_array[1]
   ) {
      limit_high = true;
   }
   /*Comment(
      "limit_low ", limit_low, "\n",
      "limit_high ", limit_high, "\n",
      "ma_low_array[1] ", ma_low_array[1], "\n",
      "ma_high_array[1] ", ma_high_array[1], "\n"
   );*/
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

16/11/22, 13:19 - Jhon Edward Sanz: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>

CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

ulong trade_ticket = 0;
bool time_passed = true;
datetime time_candle;
double last_close = 0;
double last_low = 0;
double last_high = 0;

uint MEAN_PERIODS = 715;
uint CANDLE_STICK = 60 * 10;
double VOLUME = 0.1;
double LIMIT_STOP = 500; // puntos

int ma_handler_high = 0;
int ma_handler_low = 0;
int ma_1_handler = 0;

double ma_high_array[];
double ma_low_array[];

bool limit_low;
bool limit_high;
double diff = 0;
double SPREAD = 10;
double point = 0.0;

int OnInit() {
   point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
   // SPREAD = SPREAD * point;
   LIMIT_STOP = LIMIT_STOP * point;
   ma_handler_high = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_HIGH);
   ma_handler_low = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_LOW);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}


void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_high, 0, 1, 2, ma_high_array);
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_low, 0, 1, 2, ma_low_array);

   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_close = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_low = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_high = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

   double Ask_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   double Bid_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   diff = Ask_op - Bid_op;

    
   MqlDateTime rightNow;
   TimeCurrent(rightNow);
   TimeToStruct(TimeCurrent(),rightNow);
   if (!(rightNow.hour >= 2 && rightNow.hour <= 22)) return;

   if (time_passed == false) return;
   if (!PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) trade_ticket = 0;
   if (trade_ticket > 0) {
      if (
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
            && limit_low == true
            && last_close > ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close > ma_high_array[1]
         )
         ||
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
            && limit_high == true
            && last_close < ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close < ma_high_array[1]
         )
      ) {
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket);
      }
   }
   if (trade_ticket == 0) {
      if (
         limit_low == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_low > ma_low_array[1]
         && last_low > ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         /*if (Ask -  ma_low_array[1] > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Ask - LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_low_array[1];
         }*/
         insurance = Ask - LIMIT_STOP;
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, Ask, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_low = false;
      }
      if (
         limit_high == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_high < ma_low_array[1]
         && last_high < ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         /*if (ma_high_array[1] - Bid > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Bid + LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_high_array[1];
         }*/
         insurance = Bid + LIMIT_STOP;
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, Bid, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_high = false;
      }
   }
   
   if (last_close < ma_low_array[1]) {
      limit_low = true;
   } else if (
      last_close > ma_high_array[1]
   ) {
      limit_high = true;
   }
   /*Comment(
      "limit_low ", limit_low, "\n",
      "limit_high ", limit_high, "\n",
      "ma_low_array[1] ", ma_low_array[1], "\n",
      "ma_high_array[1] ", ma_high_array[1], "\n"
   );*/
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>

CTrade trade;

ulong trade_ticket = 0;

datetime time_candle;
double last_close = 0;
double last_low = 0;
double last_high = 0;

uint MEAN_PERIODS = 715;
uint CANDLE_STICK = 60 * 10;
double VOLUME = 0.1;
double LIMIT_STOP = 500; // puntos

int ma_handler_high = 0;
int ma_handler_low = 0;
int ma_1_handler = 0;

double ma_high_array[];
double ma_low_array[];

bool limit_low;
bool limit_high;
double diff = 0;
double SPREAD = 10;
double point = 0.0;

int OnInit() {
   point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
   SPREAD = SPREAD * point;
   LIMIT_STOP = LIMIT_STOP * point;
   ma_handler_high = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_HIGH);
   ma_handler_low = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_LOW);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}


void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_high, 0, 1, 2, ma_high_array);
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_low, 0, 1, 2, ma_low_array);

   time_candle = iTime(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_close = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_low = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_high = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

   double Ask_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   double Bid_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   diff = Ask_op - Bid_op;

    
   MqlDateTime rightNow;
   TimeCurrent(rightNow);
   TimeToStruct(TimeCurrent(),rightNow);
   if (!(
      rightNow.hour >= 2
      && (
         rightNow.hour <= 22 ||
         (rightNow.hour == 23 && rightNow.min < 1)
      )
   )) return;

   if (time_passed == false) return;
   if (!PositionSelectByTicket(trade_ticket)) trade_ticket = 0;
   if (trade_ticket > 0) {
      if (
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
            && limit_low == true
            && last_close > ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close > ma_high_array[1]
         )
         ||
         (
            pos_info.PositionType() == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
            && limit_high == true
            && last_close < ma_low_array[1]
            && last_close < ma_high_array[1]
         )
      ) {
         trade.PositionClose(trade_ticket);
      }
   }
   if (trade_ticket == 0) {
      if (
         limit_low == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_low > ma_low_array[1]
         && last_low > ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         /*if (Ask -  ma_low_array[1] > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Ask - LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_low_array[1];
         }*/
         insurance = Ask - LIMIT_STOP;
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, Ask, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_low = false;
      }
      if (
         limit_high == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_high < ma_low_array[1]
         && last_high < ma_high_array[1]
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         double insurance = 0.0;
         /*if (ma_high_array[1] - Bid > LIMIT_STOP) {
            insurance = Bid + LIMIT_STOP;
         } else {
            insurance = ma_high_array[1];
         }*/
         insurance = Bid + LIMIT_STOP;
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, Bid, insurance);
         trade_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_high = false;
      }
   }
   
   if (last_close < ma_low_array[1]) {
      limit_low = true;
   } else if (
      last_close > ma_high_array[1]
   ) {
      limit_high = true;
   }
   /*Comment(
      "limit_low ", limit_low, "\n",
      "limit_high ", limit_high, "\n",
      "ma_low_array[1] ", ma_low_array[1], "\n",
      "ma_high_array[1] ", ma_high_array[1], "\n"
   );*/
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}

7/12/22, 13:19 - Jhon Edward Sanz: import pandas as pd
import os


def results_concat(path_in, path_out, group): 
    files = [os.path.join(path_in, file) for file in os.listdir(path_in) if '.csv' in file]
    df = pd.concat(map(pd.read_csv, files), ignore_index=True)
    df["group"] = group
    return df.to_csv(os.path.join(path_out,f"results_{group}.csv"), index=False)



def all(path):
    name_folder = [folder for folder in os.listdir(path) if "." not in folder]
    folders = [os.path.join(path, folder) for folder in os.listdir(path) if "." not in folder]
    count = 0
    for i in folders:
        files = [os.path.join(i, file) for file in os.listdir(i) if '.csv' in file]
        df = pd.concat(map(pd.read_csv, files), ignore_index=True)
        df["group"] = name_folder[count]
        df.to_csv(os.path.join(path, f"all_{name_folder[count]}.csv"), index=False)  
        count += 1
    fil = [os.path.join(path, file) for file in os.listdir(path) if '.csv' in file]
    frame = pd.concat(map(pd.read_csv, fil), ignore_index=True)
    return frame.to_csv(os.path.join(path, "all_.csv"), index=False)


all("C:/Users/jhons/Desktop/resultados")

8/2/23, 16:13 - ğŸ¦: .
8/2/23, 16:15 - ğŸ¦: ..
8/2/23, 16:16 - Jhon Edward Sanz: #include <Trade/Trade.mqh>
#include <Trade/PositionInfo.mqh>
#include <Math\Stat\Math.mqh>

CTrade trade;
CPositionInfo pos_info;

bool time_passed = true;
double last_close, last_low, last_high;

uint MEAN_PERIODS = 4960;
uint CANDLE_STICK = 60 * 1;
double VOLUME = 0.1;
double LIMIT_STOP = 1150;

/**
* Para controlar los indicadores
*/
int ma_handler_high, ma_handler_low;
double ma_high_array[], ma_low_array[];

/**
* controlan cuando el movimiento del precio cambia de tendencia
* de arriba abajo o viceversa
*/
bool limit_low, limit_high;

// ask - bid
double diff = 0;
double SPREAD = 10000000000;
double point = 0.0;

// Se maneja el stop loss con variables para evitar
// que el programa cierre las operaciones con el stop normal
// y poder aproximar los valores
double buy_sl, sell_sl = 0.0;

// Almacenar los tickets de las dos posibles operaciones
ulong buy_op_ticket, sell_op_ticket = 0;

double higher_close, lower_close = 0.0;
bool new_higher_close, new_lower_close = false;

uint decimals;
uint getDecimals(double points) {
   uint count = 0;
   uint i = 1;
   while(true) {
      if(points == 1) {
         return count - 1;
      }
      points = points * i;
      count += 1;
      i = i * 10;
   }
}

int round_values(double value) {
   return (int)(MathRound(value, decimals) * MathPow(10, decimals));
}

bool validate_stop_loss(double Bid_op, double Ask_op, double position_stop, ulong position_type) {
   int rounded_position_stop = round_values(position_stop);
   return (
      (
         round_values(Bid_op) < rounded_position_stop
         && position_type == POSITION_TYPE_BUY
      )
      ||
      (
         round_values(Ask_op) > rounded_position_stop
         && position_type == POSITION_TYPE_SELL
      )
   );
}

bool validate_higher_close(
   double close, double sma_high, double sma_low,
   double value, bool is_buy
) {
   if (is_buy) return (close > sma_high && value < close);
   return (close < sma_low && value > close);
}

double get_new_stop(
   double close, double spread, bool is_buy
) {
   if (is_buy) {
      return close - LIMIT_STOP;
   }
   return close + spread + LIMIT_STOP;
}

int OnInit() {
   point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
   decimals = getDecimals(point);
   SPREAD = SPREAD * point;
   LIMIT_STOP = LIMIT_STOP * point;
   ma_handler_high = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_HIGH);
   ma_handler_low = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, MEAN_PERIODS, 0, MODE_SMA, PRICE_LOW);
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}

void OnTick() {
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_high, 0, 1, 2, ma_high_array);
   CopyBuffer(ma_handler_low, 0, 1, 2, ma_low_array);
   last_close = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_low = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
   last_high = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

   double Ask_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
   double Bid_op = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
   diff = Ask_op - Bid_op;

   /**
   * Opera en el rango de tiempo
   * - Desde las 2 incluyendo las 2
   * - Hasta las 22:59 sin incluir las 23:00
   */
   datetime tm = TimeCurrent();
   datetime start = StringToTime("02:01:00");
   datetime end = StringToTime("23:00:01");
   if (!(tm >= start && tm <= end)) return;
   if (time_passed == false) return;

   for (int i = 0; i < 2; i ++) { 
      if (
         validate_higher_close(
            last_close, ma_high_array[1],
            ma_low_array[1],
            i == 0 ? higher_close : lower_close,
            i == 0
         )
      ) {
         i == 0 ? higher_close = last_close : lower_close = last_close;
         i == 0 ? new_higher_close = true : new_lower_close = true;
      }
      if (i == 0) {
         if (!PositionSelectByTicket(buy_op_ticket)) buy_op_ticket = 0;
         if (new_higher_close) buy_sl = get_new_stop(last_close, diff, i == 0);
         if (buy_op_ticket > 0) {
            if (validate_stop_loss(Bid_op, Ask_op, buy_sl, pos_info.PositionType())) {
               trade.PositionClose(buy_op_ticket, 0);
               buy_sl = 0.0;
            }
         }
      } else {
         if (!PositionSelectByTicket(sell_op_ticket)) sell_op_ticket = 0;
         if (new_lower_close) sell_sl = get_new_stop(last_close, diff, i == 0);
         if (sell_op_ticket > 0) {
            if (validate_stop_loss(Bid_op, Ask_op, sell_sl, pos_info.PositionType())) {
               trade.PositionClose(sell_op_ticket, 0);
               sell_sl = 0.0;
            }
         }
      }
   }

   /**
   * Abre una operacion en el cruce de las medias
   * 
   * si es hacia arriba, compra
   * si es hacia abajo, vende
   *
   * Pueden haber un maximo de dos operaciones abiertas al mismo tiempo
   */
   if (buy_op_ticket == 0 || sell_op_ticket == 0) {
      if (
         limit_low == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_low > ma_high_array[1]
         && buy_op_ticket == 0
      ) {
         double Ask = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK), _Digits);
         buy_sl = last_close - LIMIT_STOP;
         higher_close = last_close;
         trade.Buy(VOLUME, _Symbol, Ask);
         buy_op_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_low = false;
      }
      if (
         limit_high == true
         && diff <= SPREAD
         && last_high < ma_low_array[1]
         && sell_op_ticket == 0
      ) {
         double Bid = NormalizeDouble(SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID), _Digits);
         sell_sl = last_close + diff + LIMIT_STOP;
         lower_close = last_close;
         trade.Sell(VOLUME, _Symbol, Bid);
         sell_op_ticket = trade.ResultOrder();
         time_passed = false;
         EventSetTimer(CANDLE_STICK);
         limit_high = false;
      }
   }
   if (last_close < ma_low_array[1]) {
      limit_low = true;
   } else if (
      last_close > ma_high_array[1]
   ) {
      limit_high = true;
   }
   new_higher_close = false;
   new_lower_close = false;
}

void OnTimer() {
   time_passed = true;
}
